Nevada Shipwreck

Reuters, San Francisco, 29th - The ship Nevada ran aground on an island in the Bering Sea and sent a radio message requesting help. The Japanese freighter Oregon Maru and the American ship President Madison both heard the alarm and rushed to the rescue. When the Japanese freighter arrived, it saw that the Nevada had crashed into the rocks and the hull was broken. The wind was very strong, and the lifeboats could not move forward, causing concern that the 35 crew members could not be rescued. Later, it was learned that the crew had abandoned ship and landed safely. As for the Nevada, it seems to have been completely lost. The crew is safe and sound on Aniakchak Island.

Reuters, San Francisco, 30th - The news received here yesterday that the crew of the Nevada were safe was unfortunately inaccurate. According to a radio message from the American ship President Madison, which is carrying the survivors to Seattle, at least 32 of the 35 people on board the Nevada have drowned.

Lancashire Cotton Industry May Shut Down

Reuters, London, 29th - The Lancashire cotton industry strike has not completely ended. Although the wage agreement for weavers was reached last week, the dispute for spinners has now erupted. Today, representatives of the yarn mills and the spinners gathered in Manchester for six hours to discuss the wage reduction issue, but no agreement was reached. The mill owners agreed to reduce the spinners' wages by 15.5%, as was done for the weaving mills, but the spinners' representatives refused, still insisting on the previous proposal of a 7.5% wage reduction or 10 pence per pound. The mill owners' wage reduction notice will expire on October 15th, and the spinners claim that they will resist. The cotton industry seems likely to shut down again soon.

Public Telegrams

Telegram from Beiping: To all newspapers, it is hereby noted that the National Government has decided to temporarily abolish the Beiping Pacification Headquarters, considering the importance of Hebei's defense. A Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission of the National Government should be established to oversee the region. In addition, the National Government has ordered the appointment of Wang Shuhan, Wan Fulin, Zhang Zuoxiang, Zhang Qun, Han Fuju, Xu Yongchang, Wang Shuchang, Song Zheyuan, Bao Wenyue, Yu Xuezhong, Shang Zhen, Rong Zhen, Pang Bingxun, Shen Honglie, Tang Yulin, Jiang Bocheng, Liu Yifei, and Xiao Zhenying as members of the Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission; designating Wan Fulin, Rong Zhen, and Jiang Bocheng as standing members of the Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission; and appointing Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, as Chairman of the Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission. This order, etc. In accordance with this, all organizations were completed on the 26th of this month and officially established. Before the official seal is issued, the old seal of the Beiping Pacification Headquarters will be used temporarily. In addition to reporting to the National Government and the Military Affairs Commission for record, this is respectfully reported. The Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission of the National Government.

Telegram from Hankou: To all newspapers, Chiang Kai-shek has been ordered to be stationed in Hankou to supervise the suppression of the Communist bandits. Thanks to the joint efforts of the military and civilians, we have been clearing the path and gradually eliminating the bandits. However, in the recovered areas, everything has been destroyed. There are no houses that have not been burned, no trees that have not been felled, no chickens or dogs left, and no oxen that have not been killed. According to reports from front-line generals in the past half-month, places such as Shangcheng, Guangshan, and Gushi in Henan Province; Liu'an, Huoqiu, Yingshan, and Huoshan in Anhui Province; and Huang'an, Macheng, Luotian, Mianyang, and Jianli in Hubei Province are all like remote borderlands, desolate and without smoke. I only hear cries in the wilderness, or even tens of thousands of people, kneeling before the army, haggard and gaunt, lying stiffly on the roadside. After reviewing these reports, I am deeply saddened. I have sent telegrams to the governments of the three provinces to expedite the allocation of relief funds and food, and to send personnel to provide relief. I have also issued a notice on the reduction and exemption of land taxes in the bandit suppression areas to be followed, in order to provide stability. However, the recovered areas have been in turmoil for a long time, and the disasters are deep. There are many people waiting for relief, and the areas waiting for relief are vast. The food available for relief is limited, and the funds for relief are meager. In the blink of an eye, autumn will end and winter will come, and the thought of people freezing and starving to death is unbearable. Chiang Kai-shek deeply believes that even a loving mother cannot protect her children from hunger and cold, and that famine is the source of great chaos, and great chaos is followed by famine, mutually reinforcing each other. If we do not properly plan for the aftermath, local stability and the restoration of order will never be achieved. Therefore, I sincerely hope that all people's organizations, charitable institutions, and wealthy individuals will do their best to collect large sums of money for relief and report the amount collected to this headquarters for verification and allocation. It should be understood that on this day of multiple disasters, to save oneself, one must first save others. If the country is not at peace, how can one protect one's family? It should also be understood that saving people is not only out of compassion but also a matter of duty. We should actively participate, so that the survivors can have hope of rebirth, and that there will be an opportunity for society to recover. Fortune, misfortune, security, and danger are shared by all the people of the country. Furthermore, since the start of the military campaign, not only has the turmoil been more severe than in the past, but also frugality has declined compared to the past. Cities have become increasingly extravagant, while rural areas have become increasingly impoverished. If this continues, it will only lead to ruin, and even without foreign enemies, we cannot avoid destruction. I also hope that the leaders of schools and organizations, as well as the women's community, will organize inspection groups to personally inspect the disaster areas in batches, to understand the true situation and plan for relief. This headquarters will provide protection and facilitate their travel, so that the whole country, from top to bottom, will be aware of this deplorable situation, advocate simplicity and frugality, and restore rural areas and promote the sale of agricultural products as the goal and path for all Chinese people. I hope you will carefully consider this. Chiang Kai-shek, 30th.

Important News

Fighting Continues in Shandong, Central Government to Send Observers to Monitor Ceasefire

Jinan Correspondence: Since the outbreak of the war in Jiaodong, the central government, fearing that it would affect the overall situation during this time of national crisis, specifically telegraphed both Han and Liu, ordering them to immediately cease military action. Jiang Bocheng also came to Shandong to convey Commander Chiang's order, ordering a ceasefire first, and then discussing the aftermath. Han Fuju met with Jiang in Shahe on the 23rd and immediately issued a circular telegram that evening, reporting the ceasefire, and returned to Jinan to await the central government's aftermath measures. However, for the past week, front-line telegrams have reported that Liu's troops in Yexian are still causing disturbances and the artillery fire is still fierce. Today, I visited Jiang Bocheng to inquire about everything. According to Jiang, although the war in eastern Shandong is said to have stopped, Chairman Han reported that Liu's troops were still causing disturbances, while Liu reported that Han's troops were still applying pressure. Each side has its own story, and the central government does not know the truth. I (Jiang himself) telegraphed Commander Chiang, requesting that people be sent to Shandong to inspect the front lines of both sides. Last night, I received a reply telegram that Li Yue, a major general counselor of the Ministry of Military Affairs, and Fan Yuhuang, a colonel staff officer, have been dispatched to Shandong soon. Each side will send one person to inspect and monitor the implementation of the ceasefire by both sides in order to discuss the aftermath measures. I asked if the aftermath measures have been decided, and if the reports that Liu's defense zone will be reduced and that the provincial government will assist Liu's army with 140,000 yuan per month were true. Jiang said that if this is done, it would be a way to resolve the situation, but he has not heard of this regulation. The central government is carefully considering how to resolve this matter, as it must take both sides into account and plan thoroughly before starting. It is unlikely that the war will escalate, and the second step of the aftermath measures is the most important. Zhang Yue, Chairman Han's representative, met with Minister He (Yingqin) in Beijing yesterday and is leaving Beijing again today to go to Guling to meet with Commander Chiang. Whether Liu's unit will reduce its defense zone or be transferred elsewhere will definitely be decided. (28th)

Guangdong Province Reduces Government Expenses

Annual Savings of 960,000 Yuan

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong province has recently been facing heavy military expenses. Although Chen Jitang announced some time ago that monthly expenses would be reduced from 4.7 million yuan to 4.3 million yuan, the monthly expense of over 4 million yuan still accounts for a large portion of the revenue, making the budget still tight. Therefore, the Guangdong Provincial Government decided to reduce the administrative expenses of provincial-level institutions. If the reduction in administrative expenses is implemented, it will save approximately 960,000 yuan per year. The administrative expenses being reduced include construction, finance, education, and civil affairs. The relevant agencies have prepared standards and submitted them to the 116th Provincial Affairs Meeting for deliberation and approval. The following is an investigation of the reduced administrative expense items: (A) Administrative Expenses: (1) Expenses for each county government: The expenses for the eighteen first-class counties are 3,580 yuan per month, totaling 64,440 yuan. This will be reduced to 80%, saving 12,888 yuan per month, or 154,656 yuan per year. (2) Expenses for the Training Institute for Autonomous Work Personnel: The annual expense is 364,468 yuan, which will be reduced by 60,000 yuan per year. (3) Salary and travel expenses for local autonomy assistants: The annual expense is 69,600 yuan, which will be reduced by half, saving 34,800 yuan per year. (4) The Han River Guard Battalion will be disbanded, saving the monthly subsidy of 4,248 yuan from the provincial treasury and the annual temporary expenses of 5,000 yuan, for a total annual savings of 55,976 yuan. (B) Financial Expenses: (1) The Chaoshan District Collection Office of the Finance Department can be abolished, saving 12,180 yuan per year. (2) The expenses of the Foshan Supplementary Tax Bureau of the Finance Department are 5,604 yuan per year. It is now changed to commercial management and publicly bid for, and this expense can be completely saved. (C) Educational and Cultural Expenses: (1) Expenses for the provincial vocational school: It is found that the school has not yet been organized and will be paid for next year, saving 120,000 yuan per year. (2) The construction fee of 50,000 yuan for the Shipai Horse Racing Ground will be completely cut. (D) Agricultural and Mining Expenses: (1) The Soil Survey Institute affiliated to the Agricultural and Forestry Bureau will be abolished, saving more than 2,000 yuan per month, or 24,000 yuan per year. (E) Industrial and Commercial Expenses: (1) The Bureau of Weights and Measures will be abolished, saving 23,712 yuan per year. (F) Construction Expenses: (1) The allocated funds of 400,000 yuan for the Xicun Cement Plant will be repaid from the plant's profits, and this expense can be completely saved. (G) Assistance Expenses: (1) The subsidy to the Guangdong Office of the Hong Kong Federation of Trade Unions will be cut, saving 3,000 yuan per year. (2) The subsidy to the Party-run Poor People's Hospital will be cut, saving 2,400 yuan per year. In total, the above will save 961,376 yuan per year. (September 22nd)

Recent News on the Communist Suppression in the Guangdong Border

Communist Bandits in the Vicinity of Wuping and Xinfeng are Being Defeated One After Another

Xiang Hanping Returns to the Province, Qu Shounian Comes to Guangdong on a Mission

Guangzhou dispatch: The Communist bandits of Fujian and Jiangxi have recently been continuously pressured by the armies of various provinces. The remaining bandits are fleeing south in droves. The main force of the bandit army is still in Ruijin and Huichang in eastern Jiangxi, using Changting as a barrier. The 19th Route Army of Fujian Province has recently gone straight to western Fujian, advancing towards Changting. The 19th Route Army's Shen Guanghan Division and Deng Zhicai Brigade captured Longyan at the beginning of the month and are now stationed at Shizhong. Qu Shounian's Division is gathered at Hexi, connecting with Shen's division. On the 18th of this month, Qu's division advanced to Longshan again, while Shen's division and Deng's brigade moved from Longyan to Kanshi, attacking the Communist bandits in Kanshi and Fushi together with the 49th Division of the Central Army, Xiao Yuesheng's Brigade. In the area along the Guangdong-Fujian border, the First Independent Division and the Eighth Division of the Third Army under Chen Jitang's command are deployed in Xunwu, Shanghang, and Wuping. The Eighth Division of the Third Army has successively burned down the bandit nests and obstacles south of Xunwu. The First Independent Division ordered the Fourth Regiment of the Second Brigade, led by Li Hengzhong, on the 21st of this month to advance and suppress the local Communists in Tingtou Market, which belongs to Wuping County. At about 6 p.m. that afternoon, they arrived more than ten miles away from Tingtou and set up camp. At about 4 a.m. on the 22nd, they came into contact with more than a thousand Communist bandits in Tingtou Market. The bandit gangs stubbornly resisted from their fortified positions, and after a fierce battle for two hours, the bandit crowd

Page 12

could not withstand the assault and fled towards Taoxi. Li's regiment dispatched a small part to track down and search, while the main part remained to guard the county seat of Wuping. On the Jiangnan front, a group of Communist bandits launched a fierce attack on Xinfeng a few days ago, but were repelled. Afterwards, they continued to attack with small groups from time to time. Wang Zanbin's Division of the Gui Army, stationed in Sengfeng, specially dispatched the Pang Battalion under its command to search in Niujing on the 23rd, and found six or seven hundred Communist bandits there. After a fierce battle for three hours, the bandits could not withstand the assault and fled towards Lishi and Shuangxikou in two routes. Because the terrain there was complex and the weather was late, the Pang Battalion did not pursue them and camped in Xinniu Market to await orders. As for Sannan on the Jiangxi border, it is currently defended by Zhang Meixin's Division of the Second Army. Zhang returned to the province a few days ago to report on the border situation and flew back to Longnan defense area by plane on the 22nd. Xiang Hanping, the Commander of the Second Army, took advantage of the return of Zhang, the Division Commander, to return to the province himself to coordinate the bandit suppression plan with the local authorities. He specially accompanied the staff of the Second Army Headquarters back to Guangdong, departed from Longnan for Wengyuan on the 24th, escorted by a battalion of soldiers dispatched by the Wu Regiment of the Fourth Division. It is estimated that they will arrive in Shaoguan via Wengyuan around the 25th and return to the province by plane from Shaoguan today (the 26th). It is also reported that Qu Shounian, the Division Commander of the 19th Route Army, also arrived in Hong Kong by boat from Fujian on the 25th and will come to the province today to participate in the meeting to suppress the Communist bandits in Jiangxi and discuss various issues. (September 26)

Xunwu, Jiangnan Ravaged by Bandits

Shantou dispatch: Xunwu County is located in the key area of the three provinces of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi, with fertile soil and abundant agricultural products, and honest customs. Since the 17th year of the Republic of China, Communist bandits have been rampant, and the essence has been lost. Especially this year's tragic robberies have been even worse. Starting in March, the two groups of Communist bandits, Li Mingrui and Luo Binghui, captured Xunwu City. The guards, bandit suppression groups, and all the people's armed forces were disarmed. Party, government, and military responsible persons such as Pan Mengchun were brutally killed by the bandits. The local local Communists were even more violent. The people who fled to other villages could not make a living because they had been away from home for a long time. Moreover, the cost of living on the Guangdong border was several times higher than that of the major cities. Rice was transported from abroad and Chaoshan, costing three yuan per dou. They were not full, and they did not see meat all year round. Everyone was emaciated and looked like hungry prisoners. The people in the bandit areas who did not escape suffered the brutal oppression of the Soviet Red Guards at the county, district, and township levels. They suffered even more than they could survive and could not die. According to the latest escapees from the bandit areas, after the bandits failed to attack Fuzhou and Yihuang in eastern Jiangxi a few days ago, the bandit areas were sealed off by the National Army on all sides. The bandits are still trying to make a final struggle and are divided into two types of active work: (1) Forcing farmers and strong men to serve as Red Guards, adding a little training in running, shooting guns on mountain tops, etc., and then joining the Red Company. The Red Company is then incorporated into the transfer department's division. They are escorted to the front line to fight against the National Army. Machine guns and political companies are used behind them to supervise the team. If the forced farmers are slightly weak and retreat, they are often strafed with machine guns. Therefore, many farmers died. After the Red Guards are promoted to the Red Company, they search for strong men again and force them to fill the quota. All strong men around the age of 20 are forced to be replenished, and no one is spared. The family, father and son, know that this trip will inevitably fill the ditches, and they are heartbroken. However, under the mouths of guns and cannons, there is no way to get rid of it, and they also go sadly. (2) Extorting money and food from the people. All the people who have not escaped from southern Jiangxi whose food and clothing are enough to support themselves are designated as rich peasants or local tyrants. First, they are fined a certain amount of money, forcing them to admit this name. Those who violate it will be subjected to severe torture. Those who cannot withstand the torture and die are countless. When the fines have been paid, some people harbor grudges or slander and accuse them, and those who are sentenced to be beheaded, dissected abdomens, controlled hearts, and broken legs are also difficult to count. Recently, Deng Zihui and Zhang Guoshou, the financial commissioners of the pseudo-Central Government in Ruijin, issued 600,000 yuan of war bonds, divided into three-, five-, and one-yuan denominations. They strictly ordered the Soviet governments of various counties, districts, and townships to assign and persuade sales within a time limit, and cast hundreds of thousands of tin coins, strictly forcing the people to use and circulate them. In addition, there are so-called preferential treatment for the Red Army expenses, red aircraft donations, land taxes, and other items. The means of scraping the people are new. Good people in the bandit areas cannot escape. This is the recent measure of the Red bandits. The Red bandits in the northern border of Xunwu are stationed by the Eighth Regiment of the pseudo-Independent Third Division. Together with the local Red Guards, there are only five or six hundred people. Each person's bullets are all made by the indigenous people, with only about thirty rounds on their waists. There are also three machine guns, only one of which can be used. On September 7, the Guangdong Army Zhu Battalion Commander stationed in Niudouguang and the Yang Battalion Commander stationed in Pingyuan led troops to cover the people's regiment and recovered Jitan Market. The regiment army was only stationed in Jitan for two days and handed over the follow-up to the self-organized Shanhou by the Min Tuan Gu Le San Deng. The Guangdong Army still returned to the original defenses of Pingyuan Niudouguang. Most of the Min Tuan troops were not trained, the ammunition was insufficient, and their strength was weak. Only the Fifth District Joint Defense Team of Huichang and the Pan Jindao Department of the Third District were more combative. After Jitan Market was handed over to the Min Tuan, it was lost again after being stationed for only a few days. When retreating, more than ten bandits were killed, and the Min Tuan was not damaged at all. In the long-term red areas in the southern part of Xunwu, most of the large villages have become barren mounds. All the young men and women have been fighting each other since there were two factions, CP and AB, within the Red Bandits, and thousands have been killed. Later, local tyrants and thugs colluded with the Min Tuan, in the name of suppressing bandits, went to various villages in southern Xunwu, and abducted and sold young men and women and middle-aged women to Xingning and Pingyuan. No less than two or three thousand people have died in artillery fire during previous military suppressions. There are also tens of thousands of people who are now lucky to have the Guangdong Army Zhong Junfang, Luo Fengxiang, Xie Zheng and other regiments, together with County Magistrate Xie, adopt both suppression and appeasement measures, so the local area has been slightly calmed down. (September 26)

Xiao Lin's Mission to Siam

Related to the Signing of a Commercial Treaty between China and Siam

Shantou dispatch: There are about 1.5 million overseas Chinese in Siam. China and Siam have close relations. However, in the imperial era of 1930, the Siamese government gradually excluded overseas Chinese. For example, most of the rice produced in the country was operated by overseas Chinese. The Siamese government even proposed to take it back into state-owned management, and increased the landing import tax for overseas Chinese, at 45 baht per person (about 90 yuan). It also implemented assimilation education, requiring the principals of overseas Chinese schools to use Siamese teachers, teachers to pass Siamese language examinations, and textbooks to be reviewed and approved by the government. The severe oppression caused a rift between people from China and Siam. However, the Siamese government regarded us as a nation without a treaty. When there were major events to be negotiated, it had to be decided by our country's ambassador to Japan and the Siamese ambassador to Japan. Our government once regarded the signing of a commercial treaty between China and Siam as important. Therefore, in 1929, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent Cheng Tongsheng to Siam to investigate. The call for the signing of a treaty between China and Siam was quite high because of this, but later it subsided again. This year, the Siamese People's Party overthrew the imperial government. The leaders of the People's Party strongly expressed their pro-China policy. The representative Zhang Wutiesai said in a speech at the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Siam: There is no nation in the world that has such a close relationship as China and Siam. The Siamese nation can be said to have originated entirely from China. Examining ancient history and verifying all the things, customs, etiquette, beliefs, and habits that have been preserved, Chinese and Siamese human history are completely in line with the good friends who should coexist and prosper in the Far East and cannot be separated. The new Siamese government is now eagerly seeking to improve Sino-Siamese relations, eliminate all obstacles and restraints, and welcome the hardworking, thrifty, loyal, and gentle Chinese to Siam with 120,000 points of sincerity to jointly live and work to develop the economies of China and Siam and coexist and prosper forever. Since Siam's policy towards China has changed, in order to promote Sino-Siamese friendship, our country ordered Xie Xiang, the Consul in Penang, to take a car to Bangkok to make a preliminary attempt to discuss a commercial treaty. Before the commercial treaty is completed, a commercial commissioner will be temporarily established to promote Sino-Siamese trade. At the same time, the Siamese government also has considerable respect for the Guangdong Provincial Government, because people from Guangdong Province account for more than 90% of the overseas Chinese in Siam. Xiao Focheng and Lin Yizhong therefore made a trip to Siam. Xiao has lived in Siam for decades and is well aware of the situation of overseas Chinese in Siam and the accumulated cases between China and Siam over the years. It is said that the Sino-Siamese commercial treaty depends entirely on Xiao Lin's trip. If the result is satisfactory, Xiao Zisongjian has a good chance of being stationed as a commercial commissioner in Siam. Xie Xiang is also waiting for Xiao Lin in Bangkok, Siam. (September 24)

Journey to the West (2) (10) (9)

A Night of Startled Birds and Crying Cranes

Since Yichuan, our biggest purpose has been to investigate the waterfalls of Longmen and the coal fields of Hancheng. We originally planned to go to Hancheng via Jiyi Town and Longmen, which is about 200 li. However, because bandits are rampant on this road, the strength of a hundred soldiers cannot guarantee that no accidents will happen. So in the end, we changed our route. The first day we prepared to walk 70 li, rest in Gejiawan, and stay overnight in Gutai Street. The second day we prepared to walk 90 li, rest in Shendao Ridge (also known as Daling), and stay overnight in Yu Village. The third day we prepared to walk 80 li, rest in Xuefeng Town, and stay overnight in Hancheng, our destination. This route seemed safer, but it was more than 20 li longer than the original route. Originally, the so-called li in northern Shaanxi is divided into big li and small li. A small li is the usual length of a li, while 80 li in a big li sometimes exceeds 100 li in a small li. We have taken the road with big li more often before, and this time it is the same.

On the morning of the 7th, when we were awakened by the sound of bells in our sleep, we looked up at the sky, and the stars were still very bright, twinkling like autumn water rippling and winking at people. At the same time, the wisps of silk in the sky clearly transmitted the majestic sound of bugles, reporting that the armed comrades were also all getting up and preparing to set off. The road that day was unexpectedly lined with high mountains. Walking in the flat valley, whether on horseback or in a goose nest, you could browse the natural scenery. On the journey, you could often see clouds rising in secluded places and mixed flowers reflecting on your face. The lonely mountains and rivers rarely saw human traces. At 11 a.m., we arrived at Gejiawan, where we were going to rest.

"Can we eat steamed buns?" A tired soldier, holding his rations, sat on a stone and asked a companion. "It's best to ask the officer," his solemn companion replied, seemingly full of the spirit of obedience.

"Eating steamed buns requires asking the officer, then do you need a passport to pee?" A soldier standing in the third position jokingly interrupted the conversation, so everyone burst out laughing and the hard-working soldiers who were walking sat down and ate the rations they had like a whirlwind.

Although I was in a cowshed where cow dung was still present, covered with dead branches and surrounded by the forever annoying flies that seemed to be very energetic and flying up and down, but we enjoyed ourselves and naturally could no longer worry about hygiene and ate meat buns. At 12:30, everyone's stomachs were filled with water and food, and they regained their spirits to move forward. At that time, those of us riding horses whipped our horses and galloped like lightning. As far as the eye could see, only green mountains and white clouds quickly retreated behind us. Before 4 p.m., we arrived at Gitai Street, where we planned to stay overnight.

Gitai Street is a very small town, with only three or four shops. Because it has been ravaged by bandits several times, the desolate scene can be seen everywhere from the dilapidated houses. This is an area surrounded by bandits. When we first arrived, the truth was unknown and we were very happy in spirit. Walking in the streets where the stones were uneven, you could see the literature of the people on the walls of the houses: "A bad dream is written on the west wall, and when the sun shines on it, it turns into good luck" and "The door of the night shop opens to the west, the east wind blows the merchants to come, the south wind blows the business full, and the north wind blows a fortune." They were everywhere, and the door of the shop where we were going, which had horses and people in the same room, also had the slogan "Li Bai asks whose house is tall, Liu Ling says this place is good." The tone was still very ostentatious.

The sad wind, the setting sun, and the dark evening colors gradually came, and the sound of vigilance gradually reached our ears. Everyone inevitably became a little apprehensive. At that time, the soldiers had put on bayonets and were guarding the key points strictly. At 8 o'clock, a temporary curfew was announced. Even if one's own people went out, they needed a password. In the silent night light, the air suddenly became tense. During dinner, Zhang Mofu reported to everyone: "There are small groups of bandits entrenched in the southeast pass here. Please be careful tonight. But if there is gunfire, you don't need to panic. Please still sleep soundly and don't leave your house, because we estimate that the strength of all our armed comrades is enough to deal with them."

In terms of the situation, the location of Gitai Street is really bad. It is surrounded by high mountains, and the town is at the low point of the mountains. If a few bandits occupy the high ground on the top of the mountain in the dark night and shoot at us, we will be like fish in a pot and will only be able to wait to die. Fortunately, Battalion Commander Liu has a good plan. He first ordered the militia familiar with the terrain to be on alert at high places, while the soldiers strictly guarded the dangerous areas in the mountains. The soldiers patrolling the streets never stopped all night. The gentle moonlight shone on the dead street, which was full of fear, adding to people's fear. "Do you like the moonlight?" I asked a soldier standing at the door. They were carrying bayoneted guns and working hard for us all night. "No, no, I don't like the moonlight, because under this moonlight, we are the best target for bandits." He replied with his military knowledge. Alas, it is the same moonlight, maybe someone in the village of Riva Litan in Shanghai is praising her clarity and her beauty with a partner. Thousands of families are thinking about the cool night, and thousands of miles are covered with bright light, but here it makes people quiet and without power, and cannot get people's welcome. The object of joy and sorrow can be seen to have no certain standard. Finally, the soldier told me that the general password that night was "prosperity and strength," and the special password was "improve the countryside." Because I had nothing to do to go out, I knew it but didn't use it. When I went to bed at 9:30, I found a few places behind the house where I could avoid bullets as a preparation for unforeseen circumstances. There were also many people who slept with their clothes on and put their shoes beside their pillows to avoid being caught off guard.

Like this, we spent a night of startled birds and crying cranes, with every plant and tree seeming like a bandit. It was easy to wait until dawn on the 8th. (To be continued)

Local Communication

Taicang

The Party Department Asks for a Reduction in the Burden on Tenant Farmers in the War Zone The Taicang County Party Department recently formulated a method that tenant farmers in the war zone who have paid rent to landlords for 20 years will pay at a 60% discount, and those who have paid for 21 years will pay at an 80% discount. In addition to submitting the matter to the Provincial Party Department to consult the Provincial Government, it has also sent a letter to the County Government to submit it to the County Government Meeting for review.

Songjiang

Collective Discussion to Promote Weights and Measures On the afternoon of the 30th, the County Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting of various trade associations to discuss the issue of promoting the new system of weights and measures. It was decided that the County Chamber of Commerce would send a circular to various trade associations, asking them to purchase new measuring instruments within a week to promote the new system. At the same time, Shao Xueseng and others were sent to Shanghai to investigate the prices of measuring instruments so that they could be compared with Songjiang and allowed the stores to choose to purchase them.

Suzhou

Outgoing District Chief Accused of Malpractice Zhu Shouyi, the district commander of the County's 18th District Security Regiment, recently found out that the former district chief Tang Renjie had been involved in malpractice in the Security Regiment's funds, falsely claiming more than one hundred yuan. Yesterday (30th), he presented the evidence to the County Security Committee, requesting that Tang be transferred to the court for strict handling. The County Government is carefully reviewing the matter.

Bandit Suppression Military and Police of Nine Counties Return to Defense On the morning of the 28th, Zou Xiaogong, the County Magistrate of Wu County and the Commander-in-Chief of the Joint Defense Office of the Nine Counties in Taihu Lake, led the general mobilization of the military and police of the nine counties on water and land to go into the lake to suppress bandits. However, no traces of bandits were found in the places they passed, and they returned to defense yesterday (30th).

However, the entire county has ten districts, but only nine branch bureaus have been established. Now Zhang Yun, the Director of the County Public Security Bureau, plans to add the First Branch Bureau in Dongmen, the urban area, to be consistent with the name and reality. The Native Cloth Industry will convene the meeting immediately to establish the committee. (2) Organize a Native Cloth Joint Store under the supervision and promotion of the Native Cloth Improvement Guidance Committee.

Important Robber and Bandit Suspects Taken to Suzhou The Liaotang Public Security Bureau of the County captured a bandit suspect named Shi Jiaxing in Wangxiang. He was taken to the city after hearing that he had killed Chuan Zhongde, the Principal of Zhongxiu Girls' School in Dongting Dongshan. He was wanted. Now that the Suzhou-Songjiang Water Bandit Suppression Headquarters has learned of this, they sent personnel to Changshu on the 28th to take away the suspect Shi Jiaxing.

Wuxi

Chickens and Ducks Together Were Killed by the Butcher Chen Abao, who opened a chicken and duck shop at No. 21 Huqiao Street, Huqiao, in the city, hired two partners, one named Deng Aqi, 17 years old, and the other named Xu Maosheng, 30 years old. They have been working at the shop for two years. During this year's Mid-Autumn Festival, Deng Aqi was fired for some reason, and he was stimulated and became mentally disordered. Because he had no place to stay, he asked Xu Maosheng for help. However, at about 10 p.m. on the 29th, after the two entered the shop, Xu Maosheng suddenly shouted for help. Neighbors heard the sound and knew something had happened, so they reported it to the police. They climbed in from the Yue Dong next door and saw Aqi lying stiffly in the stove room, with blood flowing everywhere. He had already died. They went to the small loft to check and found Xu Maosheng also lying on the bed, with blood and flesh blurred and only a breath remaining. The police returned to the bureau to report the incident and sent the injured to Puren Hospital for treatment. After the police inspector inspected the scene, there were six knife wounds. Yesterday morning, the County Court sent personnel to examine the body and await investigation.

Jiangyin

Smuggled Morphine Suspect Taken to County for Interrogation In the case where the Second Jia Regiment of Qingyang Township, the 11th District, seized morphine and privately fined the monk Feng He 400 yuan, County Magistrate Ma, after learning about it, secretly instructed bailiff Wu Bowen to go to the township to arrest the monk Feng He the night before (28th) and took him to the county on the evening of the 28th. County Magistrate Ma personally interrogated him on the 29th, and after the interrogation, he was detained for investigation. However, the Second Jia Regiment absolutely denied that this had happened and defended themselves to the county.

Zhenjiang

Court Bailiff Punished for Accepting Bribes Chen Tiancai, a bailiff in the Zhenjiang Court Procuratorate's detention room, accepted 200 yuan from a certain opium offender who entrusted him on the 13th of this month and begged the court's forensic doctor to prove that he was not addicted when examining him. After Chen received the bribe, he turned to ask the forensic doctor to take care of him. However, the forensic doctor's examination was still ineffective. The parties concerned negotiated with Chen Tiancai and at the same time asked Tang, the prosecutor who was hearing the case, to be lenient in handling the case. Prosecutor Tang abided by the law and reported to the Chief Prosecutor Xu, who immediately assigned Prosecutor Tang to investigate the case. Chen Tiancai was found to have a major suspicion of accepting and offering bribes and was transferred to the Criminal Court for public trial in accordance with the criminal law. As a result, Chen Tiancai was sentenced to two months' imprisonment and fined 100 yuan. As for the forensic doctor, there was insufficient evidence that he had accepted bribes, so he was not prosecuted. The case has been finalized, and Chen Tiancai was transferred to the Zhenjiang County Prison for execution yesterday (30th).

Reward Increased for Arresting Robbers in Daosheng Robbery In the Daosheng Qianzhuang robbery in Xiwu Street, where the bandits robbed more than 2,000 yuan in cash, Zou Wenhua, the Director of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, was concerned that the bandits would escape far away because the incident had occurred ten days ago and the case had not yet been solved, so he offered a reward of 500 yuan to arrest them. Now, Lu Xiaobo, the Chairman of the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, believes that the Daosheng robbery occurred in a commercial area, and if the case is not solved, it will have a significant impact on local security. Yesterday, he specially telegraphed Director Zou, issuing another notice that anyone who can solve the case will be rewarded with 1,000 yuan in cash.

Nantong

Meeting Held to Discuss Bandit Suppression in Nantong, Haimen, and Qidong The counties of Nantong, Haimen, and Qidong have recently been plagued by maritime bandits. On the 29th, Zhang Lian, the County Magistrate of Nantong, Zhang Weixie, the County Magistrate of Haimen, Fei Gongxia, the County Magistrate of Qidong, and the commanders of the water and land police teams of the three counties secretly discussed a bandit suppression plan at the Nantong County Government. The security was very strict.

Gao Zhiwen, the commander of the First Battalion, is stationed in Rugao. Li Xiangquan, the commander of the Second Battalion, is stationed in Jiangyin. Wang Kai, the commander of the Third Battalion, is stationed in Qidong.

Rugao

Oppose the Issuance of Circulation Vouchers The Fourth Rugao County Administrative Conference decided on the 25th to discuss the proposal of the Finance Bureau and the Property Management Office to issue 150,000 circulation vouchers using the outstanding grain taxes from previous years as collateral. Yesterday (27th), the Pawn Industry, the Silver Industry, the Southern Goods Industry, and other 16 trade associations learned of this news and specially jointly wrote to the County Chamber of Commerce, stating that using the old grain taxes as collateral for these vouchers would be of no value. If they are issued, the market will inevitably be disrupted. Please ask the County Chamber of Commerce to avoid issuing them. Zhang Jieren and other members of the Administrative Conference also firmly opposed the issuance based on legal and economic principles.

Pinghu

Foreigners Purchasing Zha Pu Mountain Land

Zha Pu is an important seaport in western Zhejiang with beautiful scenery, and has long been coveted by foreigners. French missionaries purchased mountain land in Chen Shan and built a large-scale church. Although the government has negotiated, it has not been resolved for many years. Recently, there has been news from Zha Pu that foreigners have recently inspected the terrain in the Gaogong Mountain and Ma'an Mountain areas, and then persuaded a Zha Pu native named Xu to come forward. Through the intermediary Zhu Dechang, they bought more than 300 acres of mountain land owned by dozens of households, including Hu Guanhe and Liang Zhuang Township Yao Shenghe, of Changshan Township. The price per mu ranged from 30 to 100 yuan. A preliminary agreement has been signed, and a transaction date will be selected. The initial plan is to use the contract as evidence to pay the central capital donation to the respective township offices and affix a seal, and then report it to the county government for verification and tax payment in accordance with the regulations to complete the procedures.

National Central University to Open the Day After Tomorrow

Strict Measures for Student Registration and Grade Placement

Nanjing, 30th - National Central University issued Announcement A: The first semester of the 21st academic year will begin on October 3rd. Students will pay fees on the 4th and 5th, and student course selection and registration will be processed on the 6th, 7th, and 8th. Announcement B: Students from universities in the Northeast and students returning from studying in Japan who are studying at this school and have passed the screening examination will be graded and tested for their grade placement. The grading methods are as follows: 1. Those with original school transcripts must first undergo strict review by the dean and department heads. If the number of missing required courses of this school does not exceed two, they may be placed in the original grade and required to make up the missing courses. If the total number of missing courses is three, they will be placed down one grade. 2. Those without original school transcripts will be graded and tested uniformly. The courses will be determined separately. Courses that have passed the screening examination may be exempted from the test. 3. The grade placement test will be held within one week after the start of classes. Announcement C: Registration Restrictions: 1. Those who cannot register at school within the specified registration period due to illness or special circumstances and have proof may be granted leave. 2. Those who register at school within two weeks after the specified registration date will be fined two yuan at the time of registration. All class hours taken before registration will be counted as absences. 3. Those who do not register at school within two weeks after the specified registration date will not be allowed to register for this academic year and will be considered as taking a one-year leave of absence.

Educational Facilities of the Shanghai Municipal Council

Cleanliness Issues of Subsidized Schools

The Chinese private schools subsidized by the Shanghai Municipal Council should prioritize the equipment for cleanliness with the subsidy fees. However, the Education Committee intends that this equipment should only be practical and not extravagant. If the school site is rented, it is even more unnecessary, so as not to benefit the landlord in vain. In the future, when issuing subsidies, the report of the head of the Health Bureau should be considered first. After the funds are allocated, the bureau should conduct inspections at any time.

Tuition Fees for Western Parents

If the parents of students in the Shanghai Municipal Council's Western schools are not residents of the concession or taxpayers, they should pay an additional quarter of the tuition fee. However, if the parents are members of the South China Businessmen's Association or special police officers, they will still be exempt from the additional fee. The Education Committee has requested the Board of Directors to allow parents who serve as volunteer firefighters to be exempt from this additional fee. It was previously suggested that a certain number of free places be set up in Western schools. It has now been decided that this free system will be considered after it is implemented in Chinese schools.

The Question of Increasing Chinese Elementary Schools

Two members of the Education Committee wrote to the Director-General, suggesting that the elementary school near Nie Zhongcheng Public School should be opened in the spring of next year, and another elementary school should be rented in the winter of the same year. Construction of a girls' middle school should begin next year. The Director-General replied that the Shanghai Municipal Council's financial situation for next year is still unclear, and it is unknown whether there will be sufficient funds for this construction. The matter should be postponed for now.

St. Francis Asks to Continue to Be Exempted from Housing Tax

St. Francis School is unable to apply for subsidies due to the school's charter. It has requested the Shanghai Municipal Council to continue to be exempted from housing tax, to be paid from the general reserve fund. The Education Committee believes that this matter is not within the scope of the committee and should be discussed by the Finance Committee.

The Second Shanghai International Games Set for October 15th and 16th

Competition Program and Staff Determined at Yesterday's Meeting of Representatives from Various Countries

Competitions Divided into Men's, Women's, and Individual Categories; Women's Individual Competitions for Demonstration Only

To prepare for the Shanghai International Games, a meeting of representatives from various countries was held at the Western Youth Association at 5 PM yesterday. Representatives from sports organizations from China, the United States, Britain, and Russia attended. Shen Siliang was elected as the temporary chairman and Zhang Guoxun as the temporary recorder. The chairman first reported on the situation of last year's conference, and then began the discussion. The following resolutions were passed:

Walking Race Cancelled: The Chinese Walking Team requested the addition of the walking race to the International Games. After discussion, representatives from various countries unanimously opposed it, believing that since Shanghai holds an annual International Walking Race, it is not necessary to add a walking race to the International Games. Therefore, it was decided to cancel it. Competition Program: Divided into 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 10,000 meters, 110 meters high hurdles, 400 meters intermediate hurdles, 400 meters relay, 800 meters relay, 1600 meters relay, 16-pound shot put, javelin throw, discus throw, long jump, high jump, triple jump, pole vault. There will also be women's competitions, but there will be no championships or scoring. They will be for demonstration purposes only and will only have prizes. The events include 50 meters, 100 meters, high jump, long jump, 400 meters relay. Individual entries will not be scored or have championships, but will have prizes.

Scoring Method: The top four in each competition will be recorded (last year it was five), and the scoring system will be 5-3-2-1. The relay race will use the 16-4-2 system.

Registration Procedures: Individual participation requires a registration fee of 2 yuan per event, with an additional yuan for each additional event. National participation requires each country to have four participants in each competition. At least four people are required to form a group. Registration is due by October 10th. The conference is scheduled to be held at the China Track and Field Field on October 15th and 16th.

Conference Staff: Honorary President: Wang Zhengting; Awards Committee: Xu Zhendong, Cheng Yize, Fish, Bennett, Brick, Tan Yasheng, Horov, Obesongmao; Publicity Committee: Zhang Guoxun, Ma Chonggan, Xi Shunyuan, Jiang Xiangqing, Teng Shugu, Borden, Patrickov, Qin Ren, Quelostov.

Venue Staff: The main venue staff has been roughly determined: Chief Referee: Shen Siliang; Chief Inspector: Fob; Chief Examiner: McKenna; Chief Registrar: Zhou Jiaqi; Head of Track and Field Referees: Tuogou; Head of Finish Referees: Toping; Chief Timer: Rong Qizhao; Starter: Jiang Xiangqing; Venue News Reporter: Zhang Guoxun; Venue Photographer: (Undecided).

New Basketball Techniques (5) (Not to Be Reproduced) Original by Cljre Burcky Translated and Compiled by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin

The control of the center jump is the first step in basketball offense. Therefore, the tallest player or the player who jumps the highest is often appointed as the center to give the team a lot of advantages.

The referee tosses the ball upward between the two centers. The two players must stand within their own semicircles. The height of the tossed ball must be higher than the point that the two players can possibly reach. Before the ball is tapped out, neither player may leave the center circle.

After the ball reaches a considerable height and falls, each center must not tap more than twice. After that, the center may not touch the ball again until the ball has been touched by the other eight players or has touched the basket ring, backboard, or floor. If the ball falls without being tapped by either center, the referee should re-toss the ball in the same spot.

The above rules must also be followed for non-center circle jumps. The jumpers must not use their hips to bump people, push people, or use their arms to make actions against the opponent, otherwise it will be considered a personal foul.

The Arsenal Closed Yesterday

A Liquidation Committee Was Established to Work

All Factory Employees Were Separately Retained and Dismissed

Department Heads Were Transferred to Nanjing for Employment

The Shanghai Arsenal was officially declared closed yesterday. All the factory's employees were separately dismissed and retained. Regarding the aftermath, the Ordnance Department sent personnel to Shanghai yesterday to establish a Liquidation Committee at the factory, which is scheduled to start work today. Jiangnan's only arsenal for decades has thus come to an end. The details are recorded below:

Handover Committee After the factory was ordered to close, Factory Director Song Shi ordered his subordinates to expedite the handover. Therefore, most of the documents have been checked and are awaiting the committee's acceptance. It is expected to be completed in about ten days.

Employee Disposal All 70+ employees of the factory were ordered to retain or dismiss a few days ago. The dismissed ones include Long Ying, Director of the General Affairs Department, Yi Zuzu, Chief of the Accounting Section, Peng Zhenzhi, Chief of the General Affairs Section, Zhang Zhihe, Chief of the Document Section, Xiang Jingfang, Chief of the Medical Section, Zhang Zuliang, Chief of the Armory, Lin Tongyu, Chief of the Audit Section, Cao Guangyun, Director of the Material Depot, and 22 staff members. In addition, 52 employees were retained and assigned work by the Liquidation Committee. Liu Shouyu, Chief of the Engineering Department, was appointed by the Ordnance Department as a member of the Liquidation Committee. Others, such as Ma Dejian, Director of the Machinery Department, Li Chengshu, Director of the Pharmaceutical Factory, Wang Chengfu, Director of the Shell Factory, Kang Renchu, Director of the Rifle Factory, Chen Shihong, Director of the Cannon Factory, and Lin Weirong, Director of the Bullet Factory, were all ordered to be transferred to the Ordnance Department and required to report to duty immediately. The guard team was temporarily retained, and half of the public servants were dismissed. Each dismissed employee was issued one month's salary. However, the employees who were previously dismissed were issued three months' salary by the Ordnance Department, but now only one month is issued, which is unfair. Therefore, a request has been submitted to the Ministry to issue three months' salary as per the previous precedent.

Worker Dismissal The Cannon Factory of the arsenal was ordered by the Ordnance Department to extend for six months after the January 28th Incident because it was necessary to repair military supplies sent from various parties. It was not until the end of September that work was stopped. All 180+ workers were dismissed with two months' wages, except for 20 who were retained for dispatch.

Committee Establishment Since the Ordnance Department has concluded that the factory has been closed, a special person should be responsible for all the aftermath. Therefore, special personnel were sent to Shanghai to organize the Liquidation Committee. In addition to Liu Shouyu, the Chief of the Engineering Department of the factory, the committee members include Zhuang Quan, Li Shiqiong, Zheng Jiajun, Shou Changtian, and Zhou Dianli, and seven others from the Ordnance Department, who have all come to Shanghai. They are scheduled to go to the factory today to start work, take over various affairs. The office location is in the original Engineering Department of the factory. Currently, a portion of machinery, materials, unusable old cannons, waste copper, and rusted iron are still stored in the factory. The committee is responsible for the disposal methods. After the liquidation is completed, all employees will be transferred to Nanjing for employment in the new factory. As for the existing factory site, it still needs to wait for the Ministry's order to handle it.

To Discuss the Publication of the Report

League of Nations Investigation Team's Shanghai representative Tyau went to Nanjing by night train at 11 o'clock last night because the team's investigation report would be published.

The Anti-War Association Telegraphed Zhang Boling Yesterday

To Visit Han Fuju Again for Peace

The head office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War previously received a telegram from representative Zhang Boling stating that Han Fuju had stopped military actions and was awaiting a central government solution. Zhang immediately hosted people from all walks of life in Jinan to form a branch, and then went to Qingdao to form a branch. The Anti-War Association heard that Zhang had returned to Jinan from Qingdao and sent another telegram yesterday, saying: "Jinan Chamber of Commerce urgently forwards to Mr. Zhang Boling: We heard that you returned to Jinan from Qingdao. We hope you will visit Chairman Han again to maintain peace and seek solutions to avoid further misfortune. Sincerely, the Head Office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War, signed."

Zhang Qun Telegraphed Sichuan Generals to Cease Fighting

Not Only Will Sichuanese People Suffer, But International Relations Will Be Affected

Any Disputes Should Be Handled by the Central Government

Central News Agency reports: It has been rumored in recent days that Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui in Sichuan are at odds, and that they have already made contact near Chengdu. Central Committee Member Zhang Qun is concerned about Sichuan affairs and telegraphed Sichuan generals yesterday, explaining the advantages and disadvantages in order to quell the crisis and maintain the overall situation. The original telegram is recorded below: "Urgent. To Director Liu Fucheng of Chongqing, General Yang Zihui of Guang'an, Chairman Liu Zigan of Chengdu, General Deng Jinkang, and General Tian Songyao: Recently, there have been rumors in Sichuan, some saying that Chengdu will attack Chongqing, or Chongqing will attack Chengdu, or that the northern road has other plans to use force. The rumors are numerous and contradictory, but I am worried. Since the September 18th Incident, the Chinese people have been seeking unity against foreign aggression, and the international community has also focused its attention on China. Domestic disputes in recent years have already caused great pain among those who know the situation. If further disputes arise, not only will the Sichuanese people suffer, and the situation in Sichuan will not improve, but also, with the increasing external threats, it will have a major impact internationally. Thinking of the future, I am deeply worried. I believe that you all love the country and Sichuan, and you have long been aware of this. Some troublemakers may be trying to sell their tricks, creating rumors to stir up political waves. If you are not careful and fall into their trap, you will harm yourselves and the country. What will people say? I am a Sichuanese and share the same love for my hometown and country as you. I feel worried, so I must tell you. Please consider the overall situation, quell the crisis, make a joint statement to show the people of the country your great faith. If you have any disputes, you should report them to the central government for impartial handling. You must not act rashly and cause trouble. I am sending this telegram to express my sincerity. I hope you will understand. Zhang Qun, signed."

The Anti-War Association Pays Attention to the Situation in Sichuan

Divided Telegrams for Investigation Two Weeks Ago

A Reply Telegram from Liu Wenhui Has Now Been Received

The head office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War previously discussed the rumors of discord between Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui in Sichuan at the second standing committee meeting on the 12th of last month. It was decided to send telegrams to the Chongqing and Chengdu Chambers of Commerce, asking them to investigate the troop movements and deployments of both sides and to find ways to resolve the situation. Since no reply was received after a week, the third standing committee meeting on the 19th was held to discuss and prepare preventive measures. At the fourth meeting on the 23rd, it was decided to send telegrams to Liu Wenhui in Chengdu and Liu Xiang in Chongqing to inquire and ask them to reply by telegram to reassure the people. At the same time, telegrams were sent to urge the Chengdu and Chongqing Chambers of Commerce to reply quickly. On the 28th, a reply telegram from Liu Wenhui in Chengdu and a telegram from the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce were received. It is now heard that the association has sent another telegram to Liu Xiang asking for a reply. The various telegrams are recorded below: Telegram to the Chengdu and Chongqing Chambers of Commerce: "To the Chengdu and Chongqing Chambers of Commerce and all legal entities: There are rumors here that the troops of Chengdu and Chongqing are being mobilized and deployed. This association is deeply concerned about this situation, which is within the scope of our duties. We urgently hope that your associations and all legal entities will conduct a detailed investigation and inform us by express mail. At a time when foreign aggression is urgent, how can we tolerate internal strife? If something does happen, you should find ways to resolve it and provide us with your opinions so that we can work with all sectors of your province to prepare for the worst. We send this telegram to you and await your reply. The Head Office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War, signed." (Sent on September 12th)

Another Telegram to the Chengdu and Chongqing Chambers of Commerce: "To the Chengdu and Chongqing Chambers of Commerce: The telegram was sent a few days ago. We hope for a prompt reply. The Head Office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War, signed." (Sent on September 23rd)

Telegrams to Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui: "To Chairman Liu of the Chengdu Provincial Government and Director Liu of Chongqing: In recent days, Sichuanese people in Shanghai have come to our association to request that the troops of Chengdu and Chongqing are being mobilized and that unfortunate events may occur. They hope that measures will be taken to resolve the situation. At a time of national crisis, we cannot tolerate internal strife and become a laughing stock to foreigners. You are both respected and have foresight, so you must understand this. Our association believes that these rumors are not true, but we are concerned about the opinions of the public and do not want your reputation to be harmed. We dare to ask you to reply by telegram quickly to reassure the people. We send this telegram in addition to the telegram to Director Liu. The Head Office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War, signed." (Sent on September 23rd)

Reply Telegram from the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce: "To the Head Office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War in Shanghai: We have received your telegram and deeply admire your concern for the situation in Sichuan. The movement of troops in Sichuan is difficult to conceal, but the truth of the matter has not been revealed. Our association has forwarded your letter to the relevant authorities, legal entities, and newspapers and attached our opinions to fulfill our responsibility to resolve the situation. The original document is attached for your review. We will continue to report on the situation and hope that you will provide us with guidance. Sincerely, the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce." (Received on September 28th)

Public Telegram from the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce: "To General Liu of Chongqing, General Liu of Chengdu, General Deng, General Tian of Santai, General Yang of Guang'an, Director Liu of Suiding, Commander Li of Suining, all division and brigade commanders, legal entities, and newspapers: We have received a telegram from the Head Office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War, which reads (same as above). In recent years, floods and bandits have spread across the country, and the Japanese invaders have occupied the Northeast. Internal and external troubles are concentrated at one time. Therefore, the cessation of civil war is the most important task at present. All military generals are comrades. At this time of national crisis, we should release our suspicions and resist foreign aggression, not engage in infighting. Please understand this. In recent days, there have been reports of troop deployments from various parties, but the truth is unknown. However, the news has spread far and wide, even to Shanghai. How can we, the people of Sichuan, remain indifferent? We hope that the reports are false and that we will not be accused of making baseless speculations. If the reports are true, there will be a disaster. At this time of crisis, the people of all sectors can only adhere to the spirit of the anti-civil war movement, unite and passively resist. To any party, we will refuse to comply with any demands other than regular taxes, because the people's resources have been exhausted. This is also a sincere effort to promote peace and overcome national difficulties. We know that justice is on our side and we will gain the sympathy of the majority and the understanding of all parties. We only seek to eliminate the disaster and are willing to tell you with tears. We hope that the officials will express their views frankly to dispel the doubts of the public. The people of all sectors should also work hard to unite and save the situation. We express our sincere feelings and await your instructions. Sincerely, the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce, signed."

Liu Wenhui of Chengdu Sent a Telegram to the Anti-War Association: "To all the gentlemen of the League for the Cessation of Civil War: We have received your telegram and admire your words of kindness. At a time of national crisis, we should all share our concerns and work together to overcome danger and resist foreign aggression. We cannot bear to speak of internal strife. Wenhui is working to mediate and compromise. This has always been my intention, and God knows it. Although there have been rumors recently, Wenhui's commitment to peace is unwavering. I hope that these rumors are just false accusations and that this unfortunate event will not occur. Even if people do not understand me, I will try my best to avoid it. As long as it is possible to compromise and turn hostility into harmony, I will never start a war and become a leader of the rebels. I will not disappoint your expectations. I respect your good advice and hope you will understand. Liu Wenhui, signed."

The Anti-War Association Sent Another Telegram to Liu Xiang Urging for a Reply: "To Director Liu of Chongqing: We trust that you have received the previous telegram. Please reply quickly to reassure the people. The Head Office of the League for the Cessation of Civil War, signed."

War Report from the Fourth Route of the National Salvation Army

The Shanghai Support Association for the Northeastern Volunteer Army received an official letter from Cheng Changkui, Commander of the Fourth Route Cavalry of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, sent from Rehe, saying, "We are writing to inform you that our department previously sent representatives Huang Zhendong and others to Shanghai to seek assistance. We are very grateful for your full support. Kui was recommended by the Beijing National Salvation Association to concurrently serve as the Commander of the Fourth Route Cavalry of the Northeastern People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army. We immediately led troops from Ping to the defense. Now we have arrived in Rehe. We plan to concentrate the supporting troops in that area and advance to [omitted] to prepare for a general attack. The First Detachment under the jurisdiction of this route has already occupied Liaoyuan. The Liu Zhan unit of the First Detachment is now a reserve force, advancing with the headquarters. The Li Juchuan unit of the Third Detachment is attacking north of [omitted]. The Han Lingge unit of the Fourth Detachment is advancing east of [omitted]. The Zhao Wenxian unit of the Fifth Detachment is attacking east of [omitted]. The Lao Heping unit is concentrated west of [omitted] awaiting orders. The Wu Zongyu commando has left [omitted] and is attacking [omitted]. According to statistics, this route has more than 18,000 people and about 70% have guns. The current military strength has actually expanded compared to the previous Mongolian Border Cavalry First Detachment. The military region has been changed and is now under the command of Peng Xiaoqiu of the First Military Region, but the goal of resisting Japan remains the same. All reasons for Kui's concurrent position as Commander of the Fourth Route Cavalry of the Northeastern People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, as well as the history of the military region and the current deployment of troops, are reported to your association for your reference. We hope to continue to receive support in the future."

Liu Zongyao, Representative of the Northeastern Volunteer Army, Returned North Last Night

According to the China Eastern News Agency, Liu Zongyao, representative of the Twenty-Sixth Route of the Northeastern People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, returned to the defense last night at the summons of Zhang Mingwu, commander of the route, to participate in important meetings.

Conversation According to what he told the China Eastern News Agency reporter before his departure, the 26th Route and the Wang Xianting and Geng Jizhou troops have now formed a line, advancing from Tiger Mountain and Yixian County. When the guard company and the broadsword team of the Fourth Detachment encountered the enemy, they killed dozens and captured many weapons. The various routes are encircling the Jinzhou Station and are already in contact.

Declaration Liu Zongyao issued a declaration yesterday, saying: "To all levels of the Kuomintang, all people's organizations, all institutions, all schools, all newspapers, all army division, brigade commanders, all soldiers, and all compatriots: Our Central Plains is in ruins, the people are suffering, and internal strife is frequent. The situation is hopeless. The overall situation is one of temporary peace, but the Japanese are taking advantage of our disasters to invade our country, slaughter our compatriots, and implement their Korean policy to realize their Manchuria-Mongolia policy. They have occupied Liaoning and Heilongjiang, and are again invading Tianjin and Beijing. The Northeast has fallen, Shanghai has suffered a tragic defeat, and now they are invading Rehe and planning to attack North China. They are determined to destroy our China. Tens of millions of compatriots are crying out for help, awaiting death with their hands tied, suffering countless tortures and deaths, displaced and with no way to return. The country has not yet perished, but the knife is already at our throats. They are still harboring evil intentions, advancing step by step, invading and plundering, using every means possible. However, any Chinese person with loyalty and righteousness cannot but feel heartbroken. Now that the building is about to collapse, one pillar cannot support it. To preserve our nation and the livelihood of our people, we must dedicate ourselves to resisting the enemy, be of one mind and one heart, provide assistance and funds, unite our spirits, and work together to save the sinking ship. We hope that all people in the country will wake up quickly, work hard to unite, and no longer hesitate. All Chinese patriots, national defenders, wherever they are, regardless of who is being attacked, must hold the idea that there are no boundaries. The survival of the country depends on the last drop of blood. Loyal and righteous compatriots, wake up and rise up, pool our resources and efforts, and urgently seek to save the situation. We express our sincerity and await your instructions. Liu Zongyao, Representative for Assistance of the Twenty-Sixth Route of the Northeastern People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army."

Approved the Organizational Rules of the Cadre Departments of Various Industries

Appointed Representatives to Go to Various Places to Organize Branches

The Committee for Upholding the League of Nations Covenant held its third standing committee meeting yesterday on the third floor of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Committee members Ge Jiec臣, Ma Shao荃, Zheng Zenan, Ye Jiaxing, Zheng Chengqing, Xie Zhongle, Ke Gan臣 and others attended. Several important cases were resolved. Meeting Situation The association held a standing committee meeting yesterday and elected Zheng Chengqing as chairman. The resolutions are as follows: (1) Discussed the case of the directors of each department. Zheng Chengqing will temporarily serve as the director of the general affairs department, Sun Mingqi as the director of the organization department, and Li Wenjie as the director of the publicity department. (2) Discussed the detailed rules of each department and decided to hand them over to the directors of each department for review. (3) Discussed the case of appointing representatives to go to various chambers of commerce to organize branches. It was decided to appoint Ma Shao荃, Ye Jiaxing, Luo Qinghua, and Zheng Chengqing to go to various places to negotiate. It was scheduled to go to Hangzhou on October 2. (4) Discussed the organizational rules of the cadre departments of various trade associations and decided to approve them.

Letter from the German Chamber of Commerce The German Chamber of Commerce replied to the Association yesterday, expressing its sympathy. The original letter stated: "We acknowledge receipt of your letter of the 13th of this month, regarding the organization of a committee to uphold the League of Nations Covenant, based on the spirit of Article 16 of the Covenant regarding economic sanctions, and the principle of free trade for merchants, in order to deal with ambitious countries occupying Chinese territory, and to assist in introducing and promoting the sale of goods from friendly nations that treat China fairly. We have now notified our German merchants accordingly. We are writing to inform you of this matter. Please take note." (abridged)

The Continental Daily Reports a Conversation with Sakonji

The Japanese Consul General Sends a Letter to the Newspaper to Correct the Record

The English-language Continental Daily reported on the 28th that Japanese Naval Commander Sakonji had made a statement at a reception for Japanese reporters on the 24th of this month, saying that "a war between Japan and the United States is inevitable." At 2:00 p.m. on the 28th, Japanese Consul General Ishisha sent a letter to the Continental Daily requesting a correction. The original letter stated: "We are writing to inform you that your newspaper carried an article on the morning of the 28th entitled 'Lieutenant General Sakonji Declares that a War between Japan and the United States is Inevitable; Japan is Adequately Prepared.' After investigation, all the allegations are fabricated. Commander Sakonji did host a reception for Japanese reporters on the 24th of this month, but the content of the conversation was as follows: 'The Shanghai Incident this time was caused by misunderstandings and accumulated resentment between the two countries. It is very regrettable. Fortunately, the incident has come to an end. I sincerely hope that both countries will think deeply and carefully and not cause any more unfortunate incidents. The main purpose of the Japanese defense forces is to maintain peace. Military preparations should not be overemphasized, but they should not be ignored. The navy under my command in Shanghai is adhering to this purpose and will continue to do so. Leaders of the press, as manufacturers of public opinion, should sympathize with our position and contribute to the consolidation of peace in the Far East.' From this point of view, all the allegations in your newspaper are inconsistent with the facts and are extremely dangerous. We hope that your newspaper will make a correction."
