Essays

Four Types of People

— Zu'e

People's "view of life" is not fixed. Each person has their own "view of life." Even within one person, the value changes with time. Mencius said, "When blood and qi are vigorous, one should be wary of fighting; when one is old and blood and qi have declined, one should be wary of greed." Therefore, I quietly pondered and thought of four types of people.

These four types of people are: one who wants money more than life, one who wants life more than money, one who wants both money and life, and finally, one who wants neither life nor money. Analyzing these four types of people, one finds them worthy of pity, laughter, lamentation, and sighing.

The first type: those who want money more than life. This type can be classified as kidnappers, thieves, money-grubbers, and laborers living inhuman lives. They do not take their own lives seriously at all. For the sake of money, they can disregard their lives. Thieves, for example, are essentially preparing to risk their lives for robbery. As for money-grubbers, it is easier to take their lives than their money. They spend their entire lives "fighting" with money. Secondly, the laborers living inhuman lives are in a more pitiable situation. Although it can be said that they have no choice but to do so for the sake of survival, I still feel it is more accurate to say that they want money more than life. In short, this type of person is a pitiful one in society.

The second type: those who want life more than money. This type is relatively rare. Aside from those who are truly honest, upright, and do not covet wealth, those who are devout in religion can also be included. For example, Buddhists view money as something external, and the Ten Commandments of Christianity prohibit greed. They only cultivate themselves and are indifferent to material possessions and money. Although it is rare to find people of this type who are consistent in words and deeds and understand thoroughly, their conditions of belief are indeed such. This type of person does not seem to have much connection with society, except that they give a sense of shame to those who are insatiable in their greed.

The third type: those who want both life and money. Looking around, there are quite a few people of this type. From wealthy merchants and nobles to old prostitutes in brothels, they all value money as much as life and life as much as money, cherishing both equally. They want to preserve their health and longevity while also making more money and getting rich. Capitalists hire bodyguards to protect themselves, guarding their bodies as if they were important criminals. This is their desire for life. They rack their brains to extract wealth from the people. This is their desire for money. Even some nobles and important figures nowadays cannot escape this kind of behavior. Those of a lower kind, like old prostitutes in brothels, are desperate for money but unwilling to exert physical or mental effort. They also want both life and money. It has been exactly one year since the three northeastern provinces were trampled upon by Japanese soldiers. The officials who lost the territory sacrificed the country lightly in order to make money and preserve their lives. Therefore, this type of person who wants both life and money is truly the most contemptible, the most harmful to society, and the most lamentable.

The fourth type: those who want neither life nor money. This type is naturally very rare. Originally, how many people can disregard their lives and not love money? Fortunately, there is something that is barely satisfactory, which is that this type of person has emerged in China in considerable numbers. The Northeast Volunteer Army, known to society, can be considered representatives of those who want neither life nor money. They are truly "reckless" in fighting the Japanese. Money cannot tempt their hearts. They have forgotten their homes and their lives, knowing only to fight for the nation and save the country. Rising and falling, attacking and ambushing, going without food for several days is nothing. Killing the enemy is the most important thing. For a year, they have driven the enemy to desperation, causing them to be startled several times a night. They want neither life nor money. Only they can bear this burden. This fourth type of person is truly worthy of admiration and respect.

Having finished writing about these four types of people, readers, please look around in China and see which type is more numerous?

Literature and Art

On a Boat to Chongqing

— Hu Jianzhan, Xiuning

On the way from Chongqing to Chengdu, I was stranded in Leshan by rain and casually composed a poem to present to the two elders, Xichen and Shunan.

Drizzling rain on the lonely city, my melancholy deepens,

The river swells three feet, how many more journeys am I delayed?

My heart is entangled with dreams of returning home, regretting this distant expedition,

My companions are all talented, we chat late into the autumn night by the lamplight.

Responding to Elder Xi with the Previous Rhyme

Following you to Chengdu, I forge a friendship regardless of age,

Humbly admiring your virtue, I wish to learn from you like standing in snow,

The great journey rises like dragons and snakes, wild geese migrate to the south,

Filled with emotions, I cannot sleep at night, the moon outside the window is like a lamplight.

Science

Gutta-percha

— Gu Hu

The inner layer of electric wires, wrapped around the copper wire, is a rubber-like substance; this is gutta-percha. Gutta-percha's electrical conductivity is less than that of various rubbers, making it a truly insulating material. Therefore, it is used to make various electrical machinery. It also has a special function! It does not react with hydrofluoric acid, so it is also used chemically as a bottle for storing hydrofluoric acid. The newly invented free skin on the market is also a type of gutta-percha.

The composition of gutta-percha consists of carbon and hydrogen, as well as oxygen. Its method of production is to extract its coagulated liquid from the ironwood tree in the Malay Peninsula, heat and refine it, and then let it cool to become a solid. The pure form is white, and the impure form is brown. If more than 30% sulfur is added during heating, it will harden and is called hard rubber. Immersed in warm water or heated, it will become soft like taffy! It can then be arbitrarily molded into various items. If hard rubber is heated and bleached with sulfur dioxide, it will become a shiny, clean, hard, keratinous material! It can also be used to make artificial teeth, or if pentasulfide is added, it will become a red keratinous material. When rubbed, it emits a very beautiful luster and is used to make fake ox horn combs.

Gutta-percha is very similar to rubber, so it is also called Malay rubber. Because it is extracted from trees, I call it gutta-percha.

Discussion on Social Improvement: Ji Yu

—

The Problem of Improving Children's Reading Materials

The Differences Between Gods and Monsters and Bird and Animal Language

The recent discussions in this supplement on the improvement of children's reading materials have sparked debate among Cimin, Shunchi, and Shina. However, the focus of their arguments has been on the merits of "gods and monsters" versus "bird and animal language." In fact, these two points are indeed different, but Mr. Shina knows that they are different without knowing what the differences are. Therefore, what was originally not a problem has become one. The differences between "gods and monsters" and "bird and animal language" can be explained as follows:

Although "gods and monsters" and "bird and animal language" both belong to allegories, they also have differences between "pure fiction" and "semi-fiction" because of the different subjects of the allegory. The composition of a fact cannot be separated from three points: (1) subject, (2) behavior, and (3) language. If one of these three items is "realistic" or "natural," then the allegory belongs to "semi-fiction."

Gods and monsters are originally illusory and ethereal things. In the general concept of people, "gods and monsters" often contain mysterious and terrifying elements. Birds and beasts are originally real animals and are commonly seen by everyone. Therefore, although both are allegories, there is actually a difference between "pure fiction" and "semi-fiction."

Looking at the advantages and disadvantages, there are also differences. Because the former contains too much of a "mysterious and terrifying" element, it is not easy to wash away after being imprinted in the minds of children, and there is no way to prove its authenticity, which is tantamount to cultivating the power of "superstition." The latter's subjects are mostly seen by children. The behavior of birds and beasts, whether they can speak, is a fact known to everyone and can be understood as an allegory without explanation. Therefore, even if their effect on arousing children's interest is the same, there is a big difference in the use of teaching materials.

As for the teaching materials currently used, there are indeed many questionable points in the compilation of "bird and animal language." However, most of these shortcomings are due to the editors' shallow knowledge and excessive consideration of children's interests, while abandoning the cultivation that children should have in life. It cannot be regarded as "bird and animal language" and "gods and monsters" having only the same value.

Recently, European and American children's reading materials have not abandoned "bird and animal language," but in fact, they have gradually leaned towards realistic life. The teaching materials they use mostly center on society and instill civic knowledge in children through extremely detailed and trivial facts. Even the purpose of the "bird and animal language" allegory is mostly the same. In other words, the behaviors and languages recorded are all natural phenomena of humans and are commonly seen. In these reading materials, only the common birds and beasts are replaced as their subjects. Therefore, although this method belongs to allegory, it has actually broken through the "barriers of real language" and is striving towards naturalization.

The lack of children's reading materials in China is indeed an undeniable fact. If we want to improve them, it seems difficult to find another way other than to move forward on this path. (Moved to donate to the Northeast Volunteer Army)

Business Sutra

The Infallible Method in Business

— Shiben

Yesterday, my old friend Hong Zidong visited me. Mr. Hong is a businessman who works for a large foreign cloth firm on the sea. This firm is very prosperous and is a giant in the foreign cloth industry in Shanghai. Since its establishment, it has made considerable profits. Those in the same industry who compete with it often fail. Even a neighboring firm with strong capital and lower prices still falls far behind and cannot compete. I don't know why this is, resulting in such good results. Now, taking advantage of Mr. Hong's visit, I asked about the secret. He told me in detail about the special methods of the firm's business. I felt that his words could be emulated by merchants, so I recorded them.

Mr. Hong said that the manager of the firm, Mr. So-and-so, is quick-witted, has a clever mind, is flexible, and is familiar with the ways of business and the psychology of customers. When each partner enters the store, he must tell them the direction of the business and the various techniques for dealing with customers. He also said that in this era of commercial warfare, it will be difficult to win if you rely solely on the rigid and ancient method of "genuine goods at fair prices, no deception of the old or young" to respond and call upon customers. Therefore, you must open up new paths and use new scientific methods to deal with them in order to control victory. The methods he mentioned are roughly described as follows:

(1) To satisfy customers with goods, you should use the highlighting method. For example, if a customer wants to buy a certain amount of red satin, you should also take out a blue satin and place it next to the red satin, pretending to encourage them to buy the blue satin. By placing the red and blue goods side by side, the red satin will naturally be highlighted by the blue satin, adding to its beauty. The customer will surely express satisfaction, and the business will be concluded. If they buy blue satin, use red satin to highlight it. If they buy black silk, use white silk to highlight it. In short, focus on the word "highlighting," and you will be invincible. (2) Cater to the psychology of customers. If a customer says "too bad" as soon as they hear a low price, this customer must like to be extravagant. A low price does not match the goods. You should replace the cheaper goods with more expensive labels in the stockroom and then respond to the customer. When the customer hears the high price, they will surely say "good, good." (Mr. Hong also said that once, a customer bought a straight-woven woolen fabric. I offered him goods worth 1.2 yuan. When he heard the low price, he said "too bad" without even examining the goods carefully. Fortunately, the manager was nearby and immediately said to the customer, "Good goods, yes, yes, are upstairs. Wait a moment, I'll go get them." He took the 1.2-yuan goods from the counter into the back. After a while, he came out and said to the customer, "Are these goods good? 2.6 yuan." The customer kept saying "good, good" and the deal was done. I realized that the so-called 2.6-yuan goods were still the same 1.2-yuan goods. I secretly sighed at the manager's skill.) If a customer says "too good" as soon as they hear the price of the goods, this customer must be economical. You should take a very expensive piece and place it next to the cheaper goods, telling them that the other piece costs so much. Now, the price of these goods is really very cheap. When the customer sees that one piece is so expensive and this piece is only so much, the difference between the expensive and the cheap is obvious. They will naturally feel that the goods they want to buy are cheap and immediately make the deal.

(3) Give small favors to female customers. Women all like to take small advantages. Therefore, among the goods they buy, choose something small and inexpensive and give them a special discount, breaking the rules and cutting the price. A total of a few cents of savings can be slightly increased in the price of the expensive goods. If they save so much on expensive goods, they will be overjoyed and feel that everything is cheap. Or, after the transaction is completed, give them some small gifts such as handkerchiefs or soaps. They will surely be beaming and grateful. Next time, they will not leave even if you drive them away or scold them.

(4) Be friendly and courteous. This method is also important. People in Chinese stores often treat customers with harsh words and stern faces, making their faces as stiff as armor. Doing business is like looking for a fight. In this era of commercial competition, if you still use such an attitude, your business will be greatly affected. The manager understands this drawback, so he repeatedly warns all partners to be friendly and courteous to customers, making them happy, and the business will develop accordingly.

There are also creeds such as being attentive and courteous and returning overpaid money or lost items in full, which are also infallible methods for developing business.

No Way Out

Disappointment

— Yiping

In modern society, which values clothes over human feelings, I unfortunately have a relative who is a well-known figure in the banking industry. Although there are still many friends who have not encountered rubber stamps who are envying me for having rich relatives, I graduated from middle school three years ago. I stepped into society without knowing the immensity of the world, thinking that a middle school graduate could show off their abilities. But three years have passed, and I am still the same. Although I haven't starved to death, I have become inhuman, just a machine for eating and defecating. Of course, at this time, I thought of my rich relative, a well-known figure in the banking industry, with a car and a foreign house. So, I prepared several gifts and asked my wife to make a trip, because I speak bluntly and I was afraid of offending the rich, wouldn't I be breaking my own rice bowl? This was before the Shanghai War. My wife came back and told me very satisfied, "Uncle Xu welcomed me very much and hopes that you (me) will often go to his house to talk. Regarding finding a job, he said that he would call you if there was an opportunity. Before leaving, he also told me to go often and not to estrange relatives..." I knew my wife had encountered a rubber stamp, but she didn't have my three years of experience. How would she know that their sweet words were completely like the intoxicating soup of a prostitute? After receiving your gifts, they have to give you an empty glutinous rice ball in return. At that time, I also smiled it off. Knowing it was a blind cat catching a dead mouse, the poor are always the poor!

Eight or nine months of eating and defecating have passed, and I have gained many arts that were not taught in school, such as flattering, bragging, cheating, intimidating, and so on, to be applied anytime, anywhere, and to anyone. A few days before the Mid-Autumn Festival, we poor people were trying to escape this difficult situation when suddenly Uncle Xu's wife, Aunt Xu, came to our little room. I was both surprised and delighted. The rich also have leftovers to take care of the poor. I had already been assured by Uncle Xu that I would get a job as one of three clerks at some bank. I only needed to write an application to go to the office. I thought this was not a matter of begging the rich, but of the rich bestowing it upon me. So, after writing a letter of self-recommendation, I talked with my friends as if I was already a well-known figure in the banking industry, with the demeanor of a foreign house and a car. By the Mid-Autumn Festival, I had to prepare several gifts again and go on a ceremonial visit (in modern parlance) to greet and thank him, wanting to find out when I could start. I also called him Uncle Xu... Uncle Xu... as I came back.

Looking at the calendar, a dozen days had passed and there was no news. My wife went again, but the landlord was not at home. I heard that the banking figure had gone to Nanjing on business. Of course, the poor are always the poor! When the rich are unhappy, they don't even bother with you! Being stamped with a rubber stamp is still fortunate, a little favor is enough to make you feel flattered.

In despair, I felt like I was 10 yuan poorer during the Mid-Autumn Festival.

School Photos

Class

— Jian Chao

The classroom was filled with people. Apart from two or three individuals occasionally whispering, the rest were quietly preparing their assignments.

"Hey! Why isn't Mr. W here yet? Did the bell ring already?" Student S seemed a little impatient.

Page 22

"The bell rang quite a while ago. But Mr. W isn't here yet. This is really unexpected! I think he might be sick. Otherwise, why wouldn't he be here? He's never asked for leave or been late before!" E, who shared a desk with S, chimed in. "Ugh, I really don't like his class. It's so unreasonable. He always gives me the hardest questions to do, as if he's deliberately picking on me. I haven't prepared for English at all today. Don't laugh, but every time I have this class, I get a headache. My eyes are on the book, but my mind has already wandered off to the Grand Theater. If the teacher doesn't come, I'll really have to thank heaven and chant Buddha's name. Hmph, what's the use of learning this garbage? It's not like I'll be relying on it to earn a living." C joined the conversation, sounding both pleased and resentful. "Z, let's go for a walk in the back playground. Sitting in this prison-like classroom is really suffocating." The two of them dashed out of the classroom, hopping and skipping towards the back playground.

"Sigh! C is indeed a smart child. It's a pity she's too lazy to study and too arrogant." A voice sighed in regret.

"Yes! If she were willing to put her clever mind to studying, she would definitely become someone accomplished in the future. Didn't Mr. W say that? Mr. W has a mysterious effect on C." A playful taunt.

"Really? How do you know? What does C think? Everyone acknowledges that Mr. W is a talented and handsome person. Ha, ha, so C doesn't have to worry about failing English? Ah! No wonder he always pays special attention to her in class and teaches her differently from us. He's always afraid she won't understand."

"How could I not know? Let me tell you, Mr. W's cousin is a classmate of my cousin. That's what she told me. As for whether C also has feelings for him, only she herself knows. We certainly don't know."

"A series of clicking leather shoe sounds" approached from afar, interrupting their conversation.

"The teacher's here. Let's start class," a mixed voice said.

A young man in a handsome Western suit, with a pleasant smile, walked up to the podium. At the same time, he uttered a few polite words.

"I'm late today. I think this is the first time, isn't it?" He slowly opened the book, his eyes glancing around, as if observing something.

"What's the matter? C isn't here today?" Everyone's gaze focused on the teacher's face because of this sentence. "She came early, but she got impatient waiting for the teacher, so she and Z ran to the back playground to play ball."

"Then go call them both here;"

Mr. W seemed lost in thought. He didn't speak, nor did he teach.

"Teacher, please teach us today's lesson quickly. It's almost time for class to end;"

The students called out impatiently.

"Oh! Today? Let's teach the fourteenth lesson from the Second Book of Observation Thought and Expression. It's Passive Conjugation..." While he answered the students like this, his eyes kept looking out the window. A series of rapid leather shoe sounds.

"Click-clack" ran into the classroom.

Mr. W couldn't help but reveal a slight smile.

"C doesn't even know when class starts. She needs to be asked to come. What a big shot."

"That's not true. It's only because you are..." C glanced at the teacher's face with her captivating eyes. She defended herself strongly like this. However, no one could hear what she said next. Only C's mouth could be seen moving slightly. The teacher didn't show any anger. He still opened the book with a pleasant smile and became as enthusiastic as usual.

Fantasy

The Gentle and Refined Nanny

— Hong Shui

Yin'er cried incessantly in her bedding, her entire being filled with longing for her mother! Hoping that she would come quickly, her father tried to coax her with talk of buying foreign dolls. Not only did the crying not stop, but she even jumped and thrashed about vigorously in the bed. Mr. Hu was already feeling extremely bored and weary because his wife had returned to Hong Kong, and now Yin'er was crying and fussing in front of him, making him feel even more listless and depressed.

When Ah Si received a large batch of letters from the green-uniformed mailman, he was quite surprised. Only then did he realize that it was because young master Hu had placed an advertisement in the newspaper seeking a nanny.

"It is a great honor to be invited by Mr. Hu for an interview!" A young woman with a kind face and simple attire said, nodding and smiling.

"Don't be so polite! Now, I will have to trouble you..."

"A lively, innocent, adorable child is such a blessing! How old is she now?"

"Not at all, not at all. She just turned five this year. Ms. Liang, what kind of work have you done before? Where did you study?"

"I came to Shanghai from the X X Women's Normal School in my hometown to be the music director at X X Elementary School, and also taught a kindergarten class. Unfortunately, the Shanghai War broke out suddenly, greatly affecting the school, which has not yet recovered. I have been wasting away at home ever since. I am very eager to take the position of nanny! May I ask about the salary?" Her attitude was very sincere. "Ms. Liang is passionate about education, I admire that! As for the salary here, it's twenty yuan a month, including room and board. However, my child has a bad temper! She loves to cry, especially since her mother went home. She cries so loudly it's almost earth-shattering. I don't know if you have the patience to teach her? Hahaha."

"Although I wouldn't dare say that I can take on the responsibility of loving your son to what extent, based on my past experience, as long as I understand the child's personality thoroughly, I believe it won't be difficult for Mr. Hu to be quite satisfied."

From then on, Mr. Hu could still go to school to teach, and his spirits gradually improved. Yin'er also seemed to have a natural affinity for the nanny, and her temperament became gentler. After finishing her homework, she often went out to play with the nanny. Therefore, he was very relieved about everything. However, today was different. Mr. Hu lay on the sofa, smoking a cigarette and staring blankly at the ceiling. He had no smile on his face and looked haggard. Where had Yin'er and Ms. Liang gone all night? Just as he was thinking, he suddenly received a letter demanding two thousand five hundred yuan to ransom Yin'er. Mr. Hu was so frightened that he almost became a nervous wreck. He couldn't help but mutter loudly;

"How could such a gentle and refined nanny be a kidnapper in disguise? Alas! How can society be like this?"

Family Problems

A Snobbish Family

— Kang Shi

Mother Huang was over fifty years old and was a first-class old-fashioned person. Her husband had died four years ago, but fortunately, she had three sons and tens of thousands of dollars in savings. How happy she was, enjoying her old age.

The eldest and second sons were already married. The second daughter-in-law's family was rich, but the eldest daughter-in-law's family was not. In Mother Huang's old mind, of course, she was biased, favoring the second daughter-in-law very much and looking down on the eldest daughter-in-law somewhat. This was also driven by snobbery!

Because Mother Huang favored the second daughter-in-law, she assigned all the heavy chores to the eldest daughter-in-law. The eldest daughter-in-law was also very virtuous and hardworking, but unequal treatment, over time, would also lead to changes! The eldest daughter-in-law saw the second daughter-in-law relaxing leisurely, while she herself was busy from morning to night, so she sometimes resented secretly. From resentment to resistance, this was also human nature!

I remember once, the eldest daughter-in-law and the second daughter-in-law had an argument. The second daughter-in-law, used to being pampered, complained to Mother Huang. Mother Huang scolded the eldest daughter-in-law;

"Hey! You poor thing, born with a poor person's bones, cheap bones. Look at the second daughter-in-law's dowry, all mahogany furniture and jewelry. What about you? Just a few wretched things, not worth a penny. And you still want to argue, your temper is not small. If you want to enjoy life, you shouldn't have been born into a poor family..."

These words left the eldest daughter-in-law speechless, her heart felt as if it were pierced by a volley of arrows. How painful! She could only lament and weep, living her oppressed life.

In the Attic

Enticement From Above

— Xi Niao

The Solitude of a Bachelor

The bleak west wind had already used the power of autumn to drive away the humid summer. I loved to watch the beautiful scenery of the white clouds, inherent in autumn and like pieces of sheer gauze, closely clinging to the high blue sky. So, I often stood idly on the quiet B Road, looking up at the pale autumn clouds...

"Brother Luo Qing, long time no see, how are you...?"

A voice I hadn't heard in a long time suddenly came. It made me unexpectedly happy, like flowers blooming in my heart. I replied busily; "Brother Wu Ru, how are you? Our reunion is truly a stroke of fate. Where do you live now?"

"Everything else is fine, it's just that the place I live now often gives me a kind of layered enticement, which is the real trouble." Zhou Wu Ru, whom the classmates had nicknamed "Bloodhead Friend," suddenly felt distressed by some kind of layered enticement, which truly surprised me and made me feel like a baffled monk, unable to figure it out and amused.

The talkative him seemed to be encouraged by my surprised expression, which agitated his naturally thin lips. Inviting him to sit at my house for a while was said to be unnecessary, but the origin of the layered enticement was obediently and fluently told;

"I now live in a small so-called back building. Very close neighbors; in the front building lives a middle-aged couple. The disparity in stature between this couple is as comically interesting as Laurel and Hardy on the screen. The man is as thin and small as a sparrow, while the woman is as fat as a pig. The couple's feelings are utterly wonderful, they almost wish that heaven would never dawn. Ah! Brother Luo Qing! You haven't tasted my kind of life, I am often awakened from sweet dreams by their intense vibrating sounds, mixed struggling groans, and lewd giggling sounds, and incoherent mumbling sounds... which makes my weak heart experience an indescribable throbbing, and my hot blood undergoes an indescribable boiling. Alas! All kinds of threats, making me, a bachelor who has only one layer between them, feel embarrassed and awkward, and subjecting me to a lot of bad influences and bad fantasies..."

He narrated in one breath. I couldn't help but let out a smile of an unknown flavor and hastily said to him:

"This is an important problem. Don't continue to live there passively, otherwise, your health may be impacted!"

"But I can't find a suitable place to live for the time being, and there is no way to avoid it. Now I often put books that are beneficial to my body and mind, such as "Youth's Health Preservation", by my side, to resist this restless disturbance and extremely filthy environment..."

"The resistance of books can never be as powerful as that of brute force. I advise you to leave this arena, don't let your soul be muddled and your safety compromised." I seemed to be guiding him in a tone of an elder, somewhat like an order.

"The words are indeed true. Fortunately, I still believe in myself and won't act recklessly."

He seemed to have urgent matters and hurriedly made an appointment with me to meet again tomorrow and headed west.

The earth was covered by a black curtain, and I naturally thought of everything in the night world. In the surroundings of urbanized Shanghai, there are all kinds of provocative developments, even the harm of layered enticements! You may have slaughtered and poisoned many young people.

Zhang Yinsheng shall bear seven-tenths of the litigation costs, and the plaintiffs shall bear three-tenths. ▲ Yongkang Company, Yao Dakui versus Tianchangxiang Shop, rent arrears case (Main text): Defendant Tianchangxiang Shop shall repay the plaintiff 208 yuan and 7 jiao in rent. Defendant Fang Zhifen shall repay the plaintiff 200 yuan and 2 jiao and 5 fen in rent. The remainder of the plaintiff's claims is dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear one-tenth of the litigation costs, and the remainder shall be borne by the defendants proportionally according to the amount of each claim. ▲ Yuanlong Fuji Timber Shop versus Zhentai Construction Factory et al., payment case (Main text): Defendant Zhentai Construction Factory shall repay the plaintiff 6,012 taels and 3 qian and 9 fen of silver, of which 1,500 taels shall accrue interest at an annual rate of five percent from September 7th of this year until the date of execution. If they are unable to repay, Xu Chongdao Pharmacy shall repay on their behalf. Defendant Zhentai Construction Factory shall bear litigation costs. ▲ Huang Yuanhong versus Du Maolin et al., bill payment case (Main text): Defendant Cen Zhaorong shall settle with the plaintiff 1,351 taels, 8 qian, and 1 fen of silver in bill payment, plus interest at the annual rate of six percent from January 31st of this year until the date of execution. If they are unable to fulfill this obligation, defendant Du Maolin shall be responsible for settling. The remainder of the plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The defendants shall bear litigation costs jointly. (The above were issued on September 29th)

Public Notice: Second Price Reduction for Auction. This Court is executing the confiscation of property in the case of Wang Jian's kidnapping. The seized movable property was appraised and put up for auction, but no buyers appeared by the deadline. In accordance with established practice, the minimum price is now reduced by ten percent. The auction date is set for October 7th. Details are as follows: (1) Objects to be auctioned (2) Location of the property: This Court (3) Minimum Price: Thirty-seven yuan even. (4) Place to view the records: Office of the bailiff of this Court. (5) Executive Secretary Deng Zonghua, Bailiff Liu Yulin, September 29th. ▲ Second Price Reduction for Auction. This Court is confiscating the property of Xu Shengquan who absconded on his guarantee and is subject to litigation. The movable property of the debtor has been sealed up for appraisal and auction, but no buyers came by the deadline. In accordance with established practice, the minimum price is reduced by 10% of the factory price. The auction date is set for October 7th. Details are as follows: (1) Auctioned objects (2) Location of the objects: This court (3) Minimum price: Ninety-four yuan, seven jiao and four fen. (4) Place to consult the records: Bailiff's office in this court. (5) Executive clerk Deng Zonghua, bailiff Liu Yulin, September 29th.

Shanghai Local Court

Criminal Judgments Judgment on Cao Rongsheng Robbery Case (Main Text) Cao Rongsheng, for robbing the property of others, is sentenced to three months of imprisonment; the number of days of detention before the judgment becomes final shall be commuted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Judgment on Fei Xiaogen's case of death caused by negligence in business (Main Text) Fei Xiaogen, for causing death by negligence in business, is sentenced to two months of imprisonment; the number of days of detention before the judgment becomes final shall be commuted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Judgment on Chen Achen's Embezzlement Case (Main Text) Chen Achen is found not guilty; Meng Guozhang's trial is suspended. (All of the above on September 29th) ▲ Criminal Judgment Judgment on Bi Dechang Theft Case (Main Text) Bi Dechang is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for theft at the station; the number of days of detention before the judgment becomes final shall be commuted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Judgment on Chen Yuchang and others' Robbery Case (Main Text) Chen Yuchang and Wu Baiqing, jointly forming a gang of three or more persons, are each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for robbery; the number of days of detention before the judgment becomes final shall be commuted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. (All of the above on September 28th).

The costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant. Public notice is given by posting (The full text is posted in the court's display area).▲ A case involving Jiang Mingying and Zhu Ziping's wife in a dispute over debt. The court has set the date for a public hearing at 9:00 AM on October 24th. The defendant is required to appear in court on time for debate and must not delay. This is a public notice. To the attention of the defendant, Zhu Ziping's wife.▲ A ruling regarding the appeal of Gu Taotao in a case concerning the occupation of beach land (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The costs of the appeal shall be borne by the appellant.▲ A ruling regarding the retrial of Wang Lianhan and Zhang Xianshun in a case concerning boundary disputes (Main Text) The retrial is dismissed. The costs of the retrial shall be borne by the plaintiff in the retrial.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Mingchang Machinery Factory and Xu Renji et al. concerning payment disputes (Main Text) The defendants Weng Ke'an and Xiao Liangyi should be jointly and severally liable for repaying the plaintiff's goods payment of silver 964 taels, 5 mace, and 6 fen, and pay interest at an annual rate of 5% from January of the 21st year of the Republic of China until the end of enforcement. The plaintiff's claim against the defendant Xu Renji is dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear one-fifth of the litigation costs, and the defendants Weng Ke'an and Xiao Liangyi shall bear four-fifths. Provisional execution is approved in this case.▲ A case involving Zhu Deming and Qi Zhusan in a dispute over membership fees. To the attention of the defendant, Qi Zhusan. (All of the above on September 29th)

▲Civil Judgments A ruling regarding the appeal of Xu Quan and Gu Xieming in a case concerning objections to enforcement (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant.▲ A judgment regarding the appeal of Ni Boxu et al. and Zhou Wuru et al. in a case concerning elm trees (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Gao Honglin and the Shanghai 4th District Cleaning Industry Workers' Union in a case concerning contracts (Main Text) The defendant should hand over the sewage from the new house section of Dixiwei Road to the plaintiff for disposal. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by both parties.▲ A judgment regarding the appeal of Cao Yunqi and Sun Xiangji in a case concerning debt and counterclaim for the return of items (Main Text) The original judgment regarding the dismissal of the appellant's counterclaim for the return of the car purchase receipt and the portion of the litigation costs is reversed. The three car purchase receipts held by the appellee should be returned to the appellant immediately. The appellant's remaining claims are dismissed. The appellee shall bear one-tenth of the litigation costs for the first and second instances, and the appellant shall bear nine-tenths.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Zhao Shisheng and Fan Mingde in a case concerning car rental, etc. (Main Text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.▲ A judgment regarding the appeal of Dai Ruqing and Yuan Chouji in a case concerning rent arrears and eviction (Main Text) The original judgment regarding the amount of rent to be repaid by the appellant is modified. The appellant should pay the appellee 28 yuan in rent. The appellee's claim in the first instance regarding the appellant's payment of the remaining amount of rent and the appellant's remaining appeals are dismissed. The appellant shall bear three-quarters of the litigation costs for the second instance, and the appellee shall bear one-quarter.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Sanhua Company and Yongfeng Woolen Mill et al. in a case concerning compensation for damages (Main Text) The defendant should compensate the plaintiff with 3,114 taels of silver and interest at an annual rate of 5% from July 7th of the 21st year of the Republic of China until the end of enforcement. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The defendant shall bear the costs related to the compensation amount, and the plaintiff shall bear the remaining costs.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Shao Daozhang et al. and Chou Quanji Hat Store in a case concerning wages, etc. (Main Text) The plaintiff's claim and the defendant's counterclaim are both dismissed. The costs of the main suit and the counterclaim shall be borne by the parties themselves.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Gu Bowei and Cao Zhongfu in a case concerning debt (Main Text) The defendant should repay the plaintiff 280 yuan in silver and interest at a monthly rate of 1% from June 12th of the 20th year of the Republic of China until the end of enforcement. The plaintiff shall bear four-sevenths of the litigation costs for the withdrawn portion, and the defendant shall bear three-sevenths of the remaining costs.▲ A judgment regarding the appeal of Guo Zhaolin et al. and Zhang Fengting in a case concerning rent and eviction (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Wang Helinyin and Wang Amao in a case concerning divorce, etc. (Main Text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.▲ A judgment regarding the appeal of Lu Damao and Shen Juquan in a case concerning goods payment (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant.▲ A judgment regarding the case of Xu Yongqing and Cao Yanji et al. in a case concerning rent and eviction (Main Text) The defendant Cao Tingji should pay the plaintiff 126 yuan in rent, Chen Alin should pay the plaintiff 45.5 yuan in rent, Xu Fengdian should pay the plaintiff 6 yuan in rent, Shao Xilai should pay the plaintiff 60 yuan in rent, and Zou Jinfang should pay the plaintiff 54 yuan in rent, and all should vacate the premises immediately. The defendants Chen Rongji, Luo Deyue, Chen Longde, Heheguan Master, and Tongxing Tea Garden Master should be jointly and severally liable for the rent arrears of the guaranteed defendants if they are unable to pay. The plaintiff's remaining claims against Chen Alin are dismissed. The defendant Cao Tingji shall bear three-thirteenths of the litigation costs, and Chen Alin, Xu Fengdian, Feng Rongfa, Shao Xilai, and Zou Jinfang shall each bear two-thirteenths. (All of the above on September 30th)

Judgment on the Robbery Case of Cheng Xishun et al. (Main Text) Cheng Xishun and Tang Zhengxing, jointly carrying weapons, committed attempted robbery and are each sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment becomes final shall be commuted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. One handgun and three bullets are confiscated.▲ Judgment on the case of Wang Yougu, hindering a family (Main Text) Wang Youmian, for enticing a male under the age of twenty to leave the person with parental rights, is sentenced to three years of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment becomes final shall be commuted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. (All of the above on September 30th)
